    % that they will get their normal width if they fit onto the page, but
    % are scaled down if they would overflow the margins.
    \makeatletter
    \def\maxwidth{\ifdim\Gin@nat@width>\linewidth\linewidth
    \else\Gin@nat@width\fi}
    \makeatother
    \let\Oldincludegraphics\includegraphics
    % Set max figure width to be 80% of text width, for now hardcoded.

    % proper Figure object with a Caption API and a way to capture that

    \usepackage{caption}

    \let\PY@ul=\relax \let\PY@tc=\relax%
    \let\PY@bc=\relax \let\PY@ff=\relax}

    \subsubsection{We load an explore our labeled
dataset}\label{we-load-an-explore-our-labeled-dataset}

    labeld training set can be download
from:http://cs.stanford.edu/people/alecmgo/trainingandtestdata.zip

{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}59}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Create a new coloumn that contains a list with all the mentions used in the tweet}
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{mentionfinder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{n}{text} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{text}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{@}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ @}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{mentions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{findall}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{(?\PYZlt{}![@}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w])@(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZob{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{1,25\PYZcb{})}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{text}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{mentions} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lower}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{mentions}\PY{p}{]}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}mentions = tuple(mentions)}
             \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{mentions}
         
         \PY{n}{tweets}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Mentions}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tweets}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{apply}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{mentionfinder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}


    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}60}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Create a new coloumn that contains a list with all the hastags used in the tweet}
         \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{hashtagfinder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{n}{text} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{text}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{replace}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsh{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{ \PYZsh{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{n}{hashtags} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{findall}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{(?:(?\PYZlt{}=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{s)|(?\PYZlt{}=\PYZca{}))\PYZsh{}.*?(?=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{s|\PYZdl{}|}\PY{l+s+se}{\PYZbs{}\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{|}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}|[.,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{/\PYZsh{}!\PYZdl{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZpc{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZca{}\PYZam{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{*;:}\PY{l+s+si}{\PYZob{}\PYZcb{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{=}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZhy{}\PYZus{}`\PYZti{}()])}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{text}\PY{p}{)} 
             \PY{n}{hashtags} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{x}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{lower}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)} \PY{k}{for} \PY{n}{x} \PY{o+ow}{in} \PY{n}{hashtags}\PY{p}{]}
             \PY{k}{return} \PY{n}{hashtags}
         
         \PY{n}{tweets}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Hashtags}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tweets}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{apply}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{hashtagfinder}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \subsection{Cleansing the tagged train
data}\label{cleansing-the-tagged-train-data}

The untagged dataset is already cleansed in the Preprocessing.ipynb *
Removal of http and www links * Removal of hashtags \# * Removal of
multiple spaces

In addition we delete enter and tab encoding. And words that are smaller
than 3 letters.

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}63}]:} \PY{k}{def} \PY{n+nf}{clean\PYZus{}string}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} remove http and www links from string}
             \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}hl} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{(http}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{S+) | (www}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{S+) | (https}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{S+)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{text}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} remove @.. from string}
             \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}at\PYZus{}hl} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{@(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w+) |@(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w+)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}hl}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} remove hashtags \PYZsh{}.. from string}
             \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}hash\PYZus{}at\PYZus{}hl} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsh{}(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w+) |@(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w+)}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}at\PYZus{}hl}\PY{p}{)}
         
             \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}inter} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+sa}{r}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{[\PYZca{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{w}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZbs{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{s]}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}hash\PYZus{}at\PYZus{}hl}\PY{p}{)}
             
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} remove multiple spaces}
             \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}space} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sub}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ +}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{ }\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,}\PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}inter}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{}print (re.search(\PYZsq{}[a\PYZhy{}zA\PYZhy{}Z]\PYZsq{}, rem\PYZus{}space))}
             \PY{k}{if} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{re}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{search}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{[a\PYZhy{}zA\PYZhy{}Z]}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}space}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{k+kc}{None}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{return}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{l+s+s2}{emptyStringRetured}\PY{l+s+s2}{\PYZdq{}}\PY{p}{)}
             \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{rem\PYZus{}space}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

         \PY{n}{pos} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{squeeze}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{asarray}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{pos\PYZus{}tf}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}

    \subsection{Sentiment analyse -\/- Step 3 Building a
classifier}\label{sentiment-analyse----step-3-building-a-classifier}

    \begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{incolor}In [{\color{incolor}75}]:} \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} p = sum of all feature count vectors with label 1}
         \PY{n}{p} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tf\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{==}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} q = sum of all feature count vectors with label 0}
         \PY{n}{q} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tf\PYZus{}train}\PY{p}{[}\PY{n}{y\PYZus{}train}\PY{o}{==}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{]}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{l+m+mi}{0}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{+} \PY{l+m+mi}{1}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Notice that we add 1 to both count vectors to ensure that every token appear at least one time in each class.}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} The log\PYZhy{}count ratio r is:}
         \PY{n}{r} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n}{p}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{q}\PY{o}{/}\PY{n}{q}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{sum}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} And b:}
         \PY{n}{b} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{np}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{log}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{p}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{/} \PY{n+nb}{len}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{q}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{)}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} Predictions}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} With calculated coefficients we can now generate predictions on test set. Since we are trying to fit a linear classifier, the form of the linear equation is:}
         
         \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} y = mx + b}
         \PY{n}{pre\PYZus{}preds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tf\PYZus{}test} \PY{o}{@} \PY{n}{r}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{T} \PY{o}{+} \PY{n}{b}
         \PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{pre\PYZus{}preds}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{T} \PY{o}{\PYZgt{}} \PY{l+m+mi}{0}
         \PY{n}{accuracy} \PY{o}{=} \PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{preds} \PY{o}{==} \PY{n}{y\PYZus{}test}\PY{p}{)}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{mean}\PY{p}{(}\PY{p}{)}
         \PY{n}{accuracy}
\end{Verbatim}


\begin{Verbatim}[commandchars=\\\{\}]
{\color{outcolor}Out[{\color{outcolor}75}]:} 0.757196875
\end{Verbatim}
            
    The accuracy is 75.8 \% meaning that the algorithm classisfy the correct
label in 3 out of the 44 labels.

                             \PY{k}{return} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Hillary}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
                         \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                             \PY{k}{continue}
             
             \PY{c+c1}{\PYZsh{} IF MENTIONS AND HASHTAGS AREN\PYZsq{}T CLEAR ENOUGH}
             
             \PY{k}{if} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isnan}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{quoted\PYZus{}status\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Quoted}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
             \PY{k}{elif} \PY{n}{math}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{isnan}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{in\PYZus{}reply\PYZus{}to\PYZus{}status\PYZus{}id}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]}\PY{p}{)} \PY{o}{==} \PY{k+kc}{False}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Reply}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
             \PY{k}{else}\PY{p}{:}
                 \PY{n+nb}{print}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{)}
                 \PY{k}{return} \PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{Else}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}
         \PY{n}{tweets}\PY{p}{[}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{l+s+s1}{For}\PY{l+s+s1}{\PYZsq{}}\PY{p}{]} \PY{o}{=} \PY{n}{tweets}\PY{o}{.}\PY{n}{apply}\PY{p}{(}\PY{k}{lambda} \PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{:} \PY{n}{trumphillary}\PY{p}{(}\PY{n}{row}\PY{p}{)}\PY{p}{,} \PY{n}{axis}\PY{o}{=}\PY{l+m+mi}{1}\PY{p}{)}
\end{Verbatim}

    \subsection{Correlations with income -\/-\/-
PROTO}\label{correlations-with-income-----proto}

    We make two datasets income\_versus\_hillary and income\_versus\_trump,
lets see if we can make some correlations.
